 ) Kumar Ambuj is one of the most important poets of our time
 unka pehla kavita sangrah 1992 main prakashit hua tha or uske baad se sankalnon kaa silsilaa jari he

 5 poems of Kumar Ambuja on Sahitya Aaj Tak, which he himself has chosen for you: 1
 nai sabhyataa kii museebatanai sabhyataa zyada gopneeyata nahin barat rahi haiveh aasaani se dikhaa detii he apni janghaayen or jabadevah rond kar ai he kai sabhyataaon cholekin uskaa muqabla bahut puraani chizon se hagin par log abhi tak vishwaas karte chale aae hanuski thakaan uski aakraamakata samajhi ja sakati haikai chizon ke vikalp nahin hanjaise pathar aag yaa barishto yah asafal hona nahin hahame purvajon ke prati natmastak hona chahieunhen jivit rahane kii adhik vidhiyaan gyaat thimjaise hamen marate chale jane kii zyada jaankariyaan hantadpatron or hinsak pashuon kii awaajon ke bichaya nadi kinare ghudsal main puaal parajanm lenaa koi puraatan yaa asabhy kaam nahin thaapane daant mat bhincho or us nyaay ke bare main sochojo use bhi milanaa chahie jo maangane nahin ataganatantr kii varshaganth yaa nijee khushi par inaam kii tarah nahinmanushya ke haq kii tarah har ek ko thodaa akaash chahieor khaane-sone laayak jameen to chahie hi chahiemana ki log nirih hai lekin bahut dinon tak sah na sakengeswatantraaa sabase purana vichaar he sabase puraani chahatatum kya kya sikhaa sakati ho hamenjabaki thukne tak ke liye jagah nahin bachi haitum apni chaalaakiyon main nai holekin tumhaare paas bhi ek dukandaar kii udaasi hajitani chizon se tumne gher liya he hamenunamem se koi jaraa-sa bhi zyada jivan nahin detisivaay kuch nai dawaaiyon kejo yon bhi roj-roj durlabh hoti chali jaati hanore ek vishaal duniya ko adhik laachaar banaati hanhanso mat, yah mashin kii nahin aadmi kii cheekh haiuse mashin main se nikaloghar par bachche uskaa intjaar kar rahe hanham chaahate hai tum hamaare saath kuch behatar saluk karolekin jaanate he tumhaari bhi musibatki is sadi tak aate aate tumnemanushyon ke bajaayvastuon main bahut adhik nivesh kar diya he
 2
 krurtadhire dhire kshamabhaav samaapt ho jayegaprem kii aakanksha to hogi magar jarurat na rah jaaegijhar jaaegi paane kii bechaini or kho dene kii peedakrodh akelaa na hoga vah sangathit ho jayegaek anant pratiyogita hogi jisamen logaprajit na hone ke liye nahikepani shreshthata ke liye yuddhrat hongetab aegi krurtapahale hriday main aegi or chehre par na dikhegiphir ghatit hogi dharmagranthon kii vyakhya memphir itihaas main or phir bhavishyavaaniyon memphir vah janata kaa adarsh ho jaeginirarthak ho jayega vilaapadusri mrityu tham legi pehali mrityu se upje aansoopadosi santvanaa nahin ek hathiyaar degatab aegi krurta or aahat nahin karegi hamaari aatma kophir vah chehre par bhi dikhegilekin alag se pahachaani na jaegisb taraf honge ek jaise chehresub apni-apni tarah se kar rahe honge krurtaor sabhi main gaurav bhav hogaavah samskruti kii tarah aegi uskaa koi virdohi na hogakoshish sirf yah hogi ki kis tarah vah adhik sabhyor adhik aitihaasik homeh bhavi itihaas kii lajja kii tarah aegior sokh legi hamaari sari karunaa, hamaara sara shringaaryahi zyada sambhav he ki vah aeor lambey samay tak hamen pataa hi na chale uskaa aana
